msg:Before the kids start school, I went to Dayi Yunshang Resort to check in at Mulianzhuang Hotel.
I bought a package online for 999, which included a one-night private bath king-size bed room and a small hot pot dinner. The hotel is located in a remote area, but the environment is very good. There is a large lawn in the resort and a lake suitable for fishing. When the weather is good, it is quite pleasant to sit in the camping area outside. The hotel is Japanese-style, and the private bath is in the room, which is suitable for a family of three. The small hot pot is a combination of meat and vegetables, and is also served with refreshing cold dishes and snacks such as brown sugar rice cakes. The portion is enough. Except that the air conditioner in the room is a bit loud at night, the overall experience of the hotel is pretty good.

msg:The hotel that has been collected for a long time, finally came to check in. The Japanese architectural style is beautiful everywhere.
The hotel is in the Yunshang Resort. In addition to the hotel, there are real estate in the resort, as well as the walking classroom base of Golden Apple.
We booked a private soup twin room, there is a small yard outside, you can see the artificial lake opposite. The width of the bed is 135cm, which is a bit narrow for two people. Free drinks, fruits and potato chips are provided in the room, which children like very much. The service of the hotel is also very good. The staff will take the initiative to say hello when passing by. When leaving the store, Zhou Hong, the room service staff, also thoughtfully asked if you need a wet swimsuit with plastic pockets, which made this stay especially warm. The hotel can also rent bicycles, badminton and archery for free.
